<user_id>105064351558337073823<//user_id><user_name>David Gunther< /user_name>< date>
1402679365509</date>
< Rating>
4</Rating>
< Review>
I have been using this facility for several years. The staff has always been very nice and easy to work with. Elissa helped me with my current unit (I've had 3 so far) and she did a great job. The facility is all above ground and the main building is three levels high. You can have outside or inside units. The inside ones in the main building are air conditioned, and my unit on the 1st floor runs about 75 F. I used to have a 3rd floor unit and it was hotter - around 85 F, so try to get a 1st or 2nd floor unit if that matters to you.

When I first started renting, the prices were reasonable and comparable to other locations in the area. I started out with a small 10 x 10 unit until I needed more room, then moved to a 10 x 19. That was fine until the rent increases started. My rent went from $227 to $294 in about 18 months. There were no extra services, the air conditioning wasn't any better, they just raised the rent. I understand the District manager has changed and apparently likes to raise rents. In response, I downsized to a 10 x 15 for under $190. I hope the rent stays down, otherwise I will have either downsize again or move out.

For the friendliness of the staff and the quality of the location, I am giving 4 stars, but not 5 because of the rent increases.<//Review>

<text>There's a lot bums!< /text><pics>None</pics>< resp>
None< /resp>
<gmapID>0x80c2c971f16f512f:0xa1eb4b2d787d8548<//gmapID></record>
</dataset><record>
< Text>
One of the worst pet shops I have ever been to. Dozens of animals stuffed into disgustingly tiny tanks. No heaters or enrichment for any of the tropical birds. No air pumps, sumps, or any equipment for the fish tanks (which were all completely FULL of gigantic goldfish). The tanks were egredgiously overstocked and underfiltered. The reptiles had no heat source, many had no hides and were being cohabbed, which is a major NO for animals like leopard geckos, ball pythons, and others that were crammed together when I visited. There were around 10 red slider turtles left in a 3 foot long tank with less than an inch of water in it. There was only one dry area for them, all of the turtles were struggling to sit on the one dry rock under the (I'm hoping it was a heat lamp) heat lamp. No source of temperature control or filter in their tank either. The finches all had overgrown toenails and could hardly move in their cages. Around 6 rats were in each of the 3 tanks for them -these tanks couldn't have been more than 10 gallons each. ALL of the rats had scabs and bloody patches from fighting with one another. The "baby rats" cage (as it was labelled) was completely covered in newspaper, and one of the owners yelled at me when I tried to look inside.

There's signs saying "No pictures!!! No videos!!!" in every corner of the store. If the owners were really taking good care of the animals they have in stock, they wouldn't feel the need to hide what's inside their store. Not to mention, many of the animals have questionable origins. Some of the birds for sale are listed as illegal to own in the state of California, I'm doubtful as to if the owners know this. I'd say it's safe to assume so, unless they're so ashamed of their husbandry that they have to put signs up everywhere saying not to share pictures of their store.

I spent some time talking to and petting their Amazonian blue faced parrot through the cage she was in. When the lady (one of the owners) saw this, she ran over and yelled at me, claiming this bird bites. I'm not trying to call into question the treatment of these animals, but I've worked with very agressive birds before, and this animal nuzzled his face into my hand upon meeting me for the very first time. I really don't see a bird this friendly biting anyone without provocation.

After she yelled at me to stop, the lady ran around the corner of one of the aisles in the store and said something to her husband, who then came around the corner and followed me the rest of the time I was inside. Which wasn't very long, because as soon as I started to look through the goldfish tanks, he told me that the store was closing and that I needed to leave immediately. I asked why, since it was a few hours earlier than the listed closing time on their door. He just said, "No, you need to get out now."

I went across the street (where my bus stop was) and watched as they proceeded to... Not close the store. And let other customers in. For the full 30+ minutes I waited for the bus. Funny how they were so eager to close when I was looking around, but didn't seem to be in a rush once I was gone.

Needless to say, I will not be going back to their location for business. I will do my best to document what I saw and add the photos to my review.

If you've read this far and are looking for a good place to get fish, birds, and other animals, I would HIGHLY RECOMMEND Age of Aquariums in Long Beach, Reptile Factory in Long Beach and Garden Grove, Hong Kong Tropical Fish in Norwalk, Atlantic Tropical Fish in Norwalk (which sells various fish, birds, and some reptiles), and ESPECIALLY Tiki's Tropical Fish in Bellflower (which sells nearly every animal and all you'd need to care for them). These shops have exemplary quality animal care and stocking, and the owners are knowledgeable when it comes to the animals they sell and how to care for them. Please consider doing a little extra driving to support one of these businesses, they really do care about their line of work. I went into the Ramirez pet shop expecting the same, and left dismayed.< /Text>

< review>
Last time I checked (has been a while), this was "the" telescope store in the Bay Area.  They carry good amateur telescopes (not the junk you see elsewhere) with a reasonable selection of name brands, though not so much high-end and specialty gear.  Staff is  knowledgeable.  If you are getting started and want good advice along with equipment that will actually work in a useful way, you owe yourself a trip here.

< text>
I have known of Orion products since starting astronomy in my teens back in Malaysia in the early 80's. Back then Orion shipped products and catalogs worldwide. They have always been known for their superb after sales service, and this tradition continues to this day. They also offer an extremely wide range of scopes to suit enthusiast of all levels. Since moving to Los Angeles in CA, I have made frequent trips up to both their display store and warehouse. They go out of their way to help you get the scope you want, even if it is not in stock (got my showroom StarBlast for a lower price cause they did not have it in stock when I visited way back in 2007 from Australia!). Now that I live in NorCal, I frequent their Cupertino showroom quite a bit, sometimes just to chat to their friendly and knowledgeable staff. I also personally have a couple of their scopes and accessories and can attest to their unflinching commitment to QC. Even though their prices are no longer the lowest, the fact that they stand by their product speaks volumns. Oh and they produce fantastic full color catalogs packed with all sorts of useful information. Highly recommended!<//text>
